 Stella The Talking Dog may be a dog but he knows how to talk like a human
 stela kii maalik christina hangar ek spich pathalogist (speech pathologist) hai jinhone use ek customiod kii-board kii madad se bolnaa sikhaaya he
 This keyboard has 29 buttons which are made from different 29 words like come, play, look etc
 stela ko jab bhi kuch bolnaa hota he to vah is kii-board kii madad se apane maalik ko apni bhavanaaen samajhaati he
 Many times she presses the buttons of 4 and 5 words together to form a sentence
 stela jo america ke san diego main apni maalik christina hangar ke saath rahati he, aaj apane baat karne ke tareeke ke chalate internet par celibrity ban gai he
 Her videos shared on Instagram have been viewed by thousands and 4
 7 lakh se zyada log stela ko follow karte hai
 In a video shared on Instagram, Stella is seen repeatedly pressing the look button and trying to tell her boss that she can hear the sound coming from outside and see what that is
 Stella uses language differently when she's in a heightened state versus when she's calm! • Today when she heard some noises outside and wanted to go investigate, i told her we were staying inside
 • Stella responded by saying, "look" 9 TIMES IN a ROW, then "come out
 ” She was clearly in a more frantic state, and her language use matched that
 We all sound differently than normal when we're in distress, Stella included! • I'm impressed that Stella is communicating with language during her more heightened states, not just when she's calm and in a quiet space
 This shows me that words are becoming more automatic for her to use
 It's similar to when a toddler starts using language to express himself during times of frustration instead of only crying
 That happens when it's easy for the toddler to say words, not when he's still learning and it takes a lot of focus to talk • • • • • # hunger4words # stellathetalkingdog # slpsofinstagram # speechtherapy # AAC # ashaigers # slp # corewords # slpeeps # slp2be # earlyintervention # languagedevelopment # dogsofinstagram # dogmom # doglife # dogs # guarddog # animalpsychology # doglover # dogvideos # sandiegodog # catahoula # blueheeler # smartdog # dogcommunication # mydogtalks # animalcommunication # interspeciescommunication # loveanimalsa post shared by Christina Hunger, MA, CCC-SLP (@hunger4words) on Nov 1, 2019 at 1:14pm pdtvahim ek anya video main vah 'abhi-abhi-abhi stela stela dekho' ke batan dabaa rahi he or apane maalik kaa dhyaan apni ore khinchne kii koshish kar rahi he
 Stella shows us that communication is way more than just saying words! This morning while Jake was on his computer and i was reading, Stella wanted us to look at her
 • After she told us “now now now now Stella Stella look,” Stella patiently waited for us to understand what she was saying
 When i finally “got it” and told her i was watching, Stella pounced on her ball
 • Stella got our attention by telling us to look at her, waited for confirmation that we understood, then went ahead and started playing
 • Successful communication includes sharing a message with someone, waiting for them to respond, understanding their response, and responding or acting accordingly

 patiala ke gobindpura ke dalit gurdarshan singh ne bataaya ki pehle hamaara shmashaan ghat gaanv se bahut dur tha, kareeb 2 kilometre dur kheton main

 Breaking the bonds of caste and caste, people of scheduled caste or tribe and general category now attend each other's funeral
 ham ek-duusare ke gharon main bhi jate hai

 isi tarah se yah film bhi ek khoj kii tarah he, jisamen vyakti or uski pahchaan or aane vaale badlaav kii baat he

 vivaadaaspad bhoomi adhigrahan bill par modi sarkaar ne apane qadam peeche khinchne ke sanket die hai
 According to sources, the central government is planning to give states the right to enact their own land acquisition laws
 jaankaree mili he ki sarkaar sansad ke monsoon satr main hangaame ke chalate bane gatirodh ke bich parde ke peeche bhoomi adhigrahan ko lekar is bill par fanse pench ko dur karne kii qavaayad main lagi he
 In fact, the issue was discussed in detail in the Union Cabinet meeting on Tuesday
 iske baad pradhanmantri narendra modi ne paanch varisht mantriyon ko nirdesh diya ki wo aapas main baithkar tay karen ki sarkaar ko aage kya karnaa he
 Following this instruction, a meeting of these senior ministers was held in Parliament House on Wednesday in the chamber of Parliamentary Affairs Minister m Venkaiah Naidu
 is baithak main grih mantri rajnath singh, vitt mantri arun jetali, videsh mantri sushamaa swaraj or sadak parivahan mantri nitin gadakari shaamil hue
 It was made up that instead of prolonging the conflict, states should be empowered to enact their own land acquisition laws
 sutron ke mutabiq niti ayog kii baithak main suzav aayaa ki rajyon ko adhikaar diya jaae
 Those who suggested these were also bjp's allies
 khaastaur se punjab main akali dal ye kahata aayaa he ki rajyon ko ye adhikaar de diya janaa chahie
 Land acquisition is in the concurrent list of the constitution, so states can make laws
 kai vivaadaaspad praavdhaan jinamein sahmati praavdhaan or saamaajik prabhaav adhyayan shaamil hai, unhen kanoon main rakhana he yaa nahin, ye rajya tay kar sakate hai
 The state can also decide to increase compensation and provide employment to the affected family
 jabaki centre apane kaanoon in vivaadaaspad muddon ko dur rakh saktaa he
 Because most of the controversy has arisen over the removal of these provisions
 ek anya masalaa rashtriya rajmarg ke donon ore ek kilometre tak kii bhoomi ke adhigrahan se judaa he
 The government is also willing to act softly on this
 adhik sambhaavna yahi he ki centre adhikansh vivaadaaspad muddon se kinaaraa kar is bare main antim nirnay kaa adhikaar rajyon ko hi de de
 The comments darasal, ye ek raajnneetik faisla he
 The government feels that things should be decided only after the Bihar elections so that the opposition parties do not impose the BJP as being anti-farmer in this election
 duusari baat ye he ki bijepi shasit rajyon main apane hisaab se bhoomi adhigrahan kanoon bana kar jameen lee jaae taaki vikaas kii raftaar badhaane main aasaani ho
 Later they will be compared to Congress ruled states where due to tough provisions the states will not be able to acquire land
 is mudde par bani sanyukt sansadeey samiti ko teen agast tak apni report deni he
 However, the work of this committee is slow
 aise main ye sawaal bhi uth rahe hai ki kya is samiti ke kaarykaal ko phir badhaane kii maang to nahin uth jaaegi
 In this case, the Land Acquisition Bill will be completely averted in this session and in the wake of Bihar elections, a major headache of the government can be overcome
 darasal, mangalvaar ko kendriya mantrimandal kii baithak main is mudde par vistaar se charchaa kii gai
 After this, Prime Minister Narendra Modi instructed five senior ministers to sit together and decide what the government has to do next
 is nirdesh ke baad buudhvaar ko sansad bhawan main sansadeey kaary mantri em venkaiya naidu ke kaksh main in varisht mantriyon kii baithak hui
 Home Minister Rajnath Singh, Finance Minister Arun Jaitley, Foreign Minister Sushma Swaraj and Road Transport Minister Nitin Gadkari attended the meeting
 ye man banaaya gaya ki takaraav lanbaa khinchne ke bajaae rajyon ko apane bhoomi adhigrahan kaanoon banane kaa adhikaar de diya jaae
 According to sources, the suggestion came in the meeting of NITI Aayog that states should be empowered
 ye suzav dene waalon main bijepi ke sahyogi dal bhi shaamil the
 Especially in Punjab, the Akali Dal has been saying that these rights should be given to the states
 bhoomi adhigrahan samvidhan kii samavarti suchi main he isliye rajya kaanoon bana sakate hai
 Many controversial provisions, including consent provisions and social impact studies, can be decided by the states whether to put them into law
 saath hi muaavze ko badhaane or prabhavit parivaar ko rojgaar dene kaa faisla bhi rajya kar sakate hai
 While the Center can keep its laws away from these controversial issues
 kyonki sabase zyada vivaad inhen praavdhaanon ko hataane par hua he
 Another issue relates to the acquisition of land up to one kilometer on both sides of the national highway
 sarkaar is par bhi narmi baratane ko taiyaar he
 It is more likely that the center should leave the most controversial issues and give the right to final decision in this regard to the states
 tippaniyan Actually, this is a political decision
 sarkaar ko lag rahaa he ki bihar chunaav ke baad hi baaten tay hon taaki vipakshi partiyaan is chunaav main bijepi par kisaan virdohi hone kaa thappa na laga saken
 The second thing is that land should be enacted in the BJP ruled states by making land acquisition laws on their own so that it can be easy to increase the pace of development
 baad main unki tulana congress shasit rajyon se kii ja sakegi jahaan kathin praavdhaanon ke chalate rajya bhoomi adhigrahit nahin kar paaenge

 The instant messaging app whastsapp was not advertised until now, but will be available now
 fasebuk ne yah saaf kar diya he ki 2020 se whatsapp main aid dikhaae jaaenge
 However, this was already foreseen, as Mark Zuckerberg pointed it out
 whatsapp ke founders ko ye katai pasand nahin tha, lekin unhone company pehle hi chhod di he
 During the annual marketing summit in the Netherlands, Facebook has stated that advertisements will start appearing on whatsapp in 2020
 shuruyaat main company kaa plan ye he ki yugers ko whatsapp story section main vigyaapan dikhaae jaaenge
 Such advertisements have already been launched in Instagram
 is event ke dauraan company ne udhaaharan bhi dikhaaya he ki kaise vigyaapan die jaaenge
 During this demo it has also been reported that the ads will appear on the full screen and will be accompanied by a link
 inhen swip karke sidhe aap website par ja sakate hai
 Actually, these ads also appear on Instagram and will now work on whatsapp as well
 fasebuk ne jab whatsapp kaa adhigrahan kiya tha tab kaha gaya tha ki watsap puri tarah se independent hoga, lekin baad main dhire dhire watsap par fasebuk kaa kabja hota gaya
 After a few conferences, both founders of whatsapp left the company
 ab fasebuk watsap, massenger or instagram ko mila kar cross plateform miseging banane kii taiyaari kii ja rahi he
 Recently a new feature has come in whatsapp beta, under which whatsapp status can be shared directly on Facebook
 centre sarkaar kaa daawa he ki senetary napkin par jiesti ke antargat tay kii gai kar kii dar pehle se kam he

 parantu yah vitt varsh 2016
 Started at 17
 mantralay se praapt jaankaree ke anusaar, "nai manzil yojana ke adheen kul aavanton 155 karod rupee he lekin koi dhanrashi abhi tak jari nahin kii gai he or abhi tak koi vaastavik satyaapan nahin kiya gaya he
 " ullekhneey he ki is pariyojna ke tahat alpsankhyak yuvaaon kii shiksha or unke kaushal vikaas kii disha main ek ekikrut evam samgr drushtikon apanaaya gaya he taaki badi sankhya main alpsankhyak samudaay ke yuvaaon dwaara apni padhai bich main hi chhod dene or unke bich berogari kii unchi dar kii samasyaon se nijaat pai ja sake
 This project will mainly benefit minority youth who are below the poverty line (BPL) and whose age ranges from 17 years to 35 years

 ) Former Indian batsman VVS Laxman believes that Suresh Raina will have to devise a special strategy to face short pitch balls
 unako is samasya kaa hal dhundhna hi hoga
 Laxman is also confident that Raina will be able to come back by working hard
 lakshmana ne buudhvaar ko pitiai se kaha, ‘‘mujhe lagata he ki prayek ballebaaj ke liye koi naa koi kshetra chintaa kii baat hota he
 Suresh Raina has struggled against short pitch balls for a long time, but i think he should have a strategy against short balls and hope that he will stick to it
 ’’tippaniyan Hyderabad's star batsman Laxman said that no batsman is perfect and Raina is not the only one who has a problem with his technique
 raina ko bhale hi australia daure ke liye bhartiya vanade team se baahar kar diya gaya he, lekin lakshmana ko yakeen he ki yah jhatka unhen or kadi mehnat karne ke liye prerit karegaa
 He said, "we have seen that Virat Kohli and Rohit Sharma have had trouble on the balls going out of the off stump and Cheteshwar Pujara has a problem on the incoming ball
 sabhi kii apni apni samasya hoti he, kyonki koi bhi ballebaaj parfect nahin hota
 Therefore, Raina needs to be very clear while facing the short ball

 bas, phir kya tha

 or phir ant main, jab billi apane dost vaali 'jail' main pahunch jaati he, tab uske swaagat ke liye pille kaa josh or dost ke liye apnaapan dekhte hi banataa he, jise aap khud hi dekhen, to behatar hoga
